Two Australians remained in Uruguay as they remained in intensive care at a hospital.<ref name="mortimer.reuters" />  Passengers of other nationalities also remained on board the ship pending negotiations with their home countries.<ref name="mortimer.reuters" />

=== ''Pride of America'' === <!-- 2020.04.08: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->
The [[Hawaii Department of Transportation]] reported on 8 April 2020 that six crew members of MS<!-- standard is to include a ship prefix the first time it is mentioned in the section devoted to the ship if the ship's own wikipedia page mentions the prefix in the preface, and to omit the prefix in all other instances --> {{ship||Pride of America}} had tested positive for coronavirus.<ref name="pride.hidot">{{cite web|url=http://hidot.hawaii.gov/blog/2020/04/08/six-covid-19-cases-confirmed-on-the-pride-of-america |title=Department of Transportation &#124; Six COVID-19 cases confirmed on the Pride of America |publisher=Hidot.hawaii.gov |accessdate=2020-04-12}}</ref>  Two of the crew members were taken to a hospital for treatment, while the other patients were isolated on board the ship.<ref name="pride.hidot"/>  Another positive case was later announced, bringing the total number of cases to seven.<ref name="pride.staradvertiser">{{cite web|url=https://www.staradvertiser.com/2020/04/09/breaking-news/4-oahu-residents-to-disembark-pacific-princess-cruise-ship-at-honolulu-harbor-on-monday/ |title=4 Oahu residents to leave Pacific Princess at Honolulu Harbor Monday; 7 Pride of America crew members have COVID-19 &#124; Honolulu Star-Advertiser |publisher=Staradvertiser.com |accessdate=2020-04-12}}</ref>

Following the suspension of cruise operations to mitigate the effect of the pandemic, ''Pride of America'' has not carried passengers since 14 March 2020, and is currently docked at [[Honolulu Harbor]], its home base, with a complement of roughly 500 crew members.<ref name="pride.hidot"/>  It is scheduled to travel to the mainland to enter dry dock with about 200 crew members, with the other 300 crew members heading directly back to their home states.<ref name="pride.staradvertiser"/>

=== ''Celebrity Flora'' === <!-- 2020.04.14: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

The Provincial Emergency Operations Committee in the [[Galápagos Islands]] of [[Ecuador]] reported on 14 April 2020 that 69 crew members of {{ship||Celebrity Flora}} were tested, and 48 tests returned positive for coronavirus.<ref name="flora.twitter">{{cite web|url=https://twitter.com/CGGalapagos/status/1250198294904651776 |author=@CGGalapagos |title=🇸🇱 El Comité de Operaciones de Emergencia Provincial informa a la comunidad respecto al procesamiento de muestras y pruebas COVID en Galápagos y a la situación en el barco Celebrity Flora. 👇#ActivadosPorLaSalud #JuntosPorGalápagos |publisher=twitter.com |date=2020-04-14 |accessdate=2020-04-25}}</ref>  The positive crew members remained isolated on board the ship, located at [[Baltra Island]].<ref name="flora.twitter" />  The new cases increased the total case count of the islands to 72.<ref name="flora.twitter" />

=== ''Monarch'' === <!-- 2020.04.19: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On 14 March, Panama repatriated 1,504 Colombian tourists from the cruise ship {{ship|MS|Monarch||6}}.  Since the port of [[Cartagena, Colombia]], was closed, the people had to fly from [[Colón, Panama]]. About 300 people were still waiting to buy tickets.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.msn.com/es-mx/noticias/mundo/panam%c3%a1-repatria-a-turistas-de-crucero-por-nuevo-coronavirus/ar-BB11c7oo |trans-title=Panama repatriates cruise tourists for new coronavirus |title=Panamá repatria a turistas de crucero por nuevo coronavirus |language=es |work=AFP/MSN Noticias |date=14 March 2020 |access-date=15 March 2020 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200315170847/https://www.msn.com/es-mx/noticias/mundo/panam%c3%a1-repatria-a-turistas-de-crucero-por-nuevo-coronavirus/ar-BB11c7oo |archive-date=15 March 2020 |url-status=live }}</ref>

On 17 April 2020, a Honduran crew member died of the virus in a hospital in [[Panama City]].<ref name="monarch.crew">[https://web.archive.org/web/20200419230651/https://crew-center.com/memoriam-cruise-ship-crew-members-lost-covid-19-pandemic Cruise Ship Crew Members Lost in COVID-19 Pandemic] CrewCenter 7 April 2020</ref>  He had been [[medical evacuation|medically evacuated]] after having trouble breathing, and tested positive at the hospital.<ref name="monarch.crew" />

=== ''Costa Atlantica'' === <!-- 2020.04.20: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->
[[File:Costa Atlantica DSC09523.JPG|thumb|''Costa Atlantica'' in 2009]]

On 20 April 2020, a positive case was reported aboard {{ship||Costa Atlantica}},{{efn|Some sources reported a positive case aboard a ship called "''Costa Atranchica''", but these sources appear to be from countries that do not have a significant population that is familiar with the Japanese language, and may be mistranslating the [[transcription into Japanese|Japanese transcription]] of ''Costa Atlantica'' (either 「コスタ・アトランティカ」 or 「コスタ・アトランチカ」) by [[transliteration]] of the "ラ" as "ra" instead of "la" and the "チ" as "chi" instead of "ti".<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.cnn.com/world/live-news/coronavirus-pandemic-04-20-20-intl/h_87a531d5bd4367275a25935aa7bd89aa |title=Crew member on Italian cruise ship has tested positive with Covid-19 |publisher=Cnn.com |date=2020-04-20 |accessdate=2020-04-25}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://portnews.ru/news/294783/ |title=Член экипажа итальянского круизного судна в порту Нагасаки инфицирован COVID-19 |publisher=Portnews.ru |accessdate=2020-04-25}}</ref>}} currently docked at the [[Koyagi, Nagasaki|Koyagi]] Factory of {{ill|Mitsubishi Heavy Industries Nagasaki Shipyard|ja|三菱重工業長崎造船所}} in [[Nagasaki]] where it was under repairs from 20 February to 25 March 2020.{{efn|The ship was originally scheduled for repairs in China, but the repair order was transferred to [[Mitsubishi Heavy Industries]] after the [[COVID-19 pandemic in mainland China|pandemic began in China]].<ref name="atlantica.abscbn" />}}<ref name="atlantica.yahoo">{{cite web |url=https://headlines.yahoo.co.jp/hl?a=20200420-00010005-ncctv-l42 |title=長崎造船所香焼工場停泊客船の乗船者がコロナ感染（長崎文化放送） – Yahoo!ニュース |publisher=Headlines.yahoo.co.jp |accessdate=2020-04-25 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200426222338/https://headlines.yahoo.co.jp/hl?a=20200420-00010005-ncctv-l42 |archive-date=26 April 2020 |url-status=dead }}</ref>  A doctor had collected samples from four suspected cases and conducted [[polymerase chain reaction|PCR]] [[COVID-19 testing|tests]], with three negative results and one positive.<ref name="atlantica.yahoo" />  The positive case had suffered a fever beginning on 14 April 2020.<ref name="atlantica.yahoo" />  About 20 other crew members had started developing fevers in the week before the first case was reported.<ref name="atlantica.abscbn">{{cite web|url=https://news.abs-cbn.com/overseas/04/21/20/1-crew-member-tests-positive-20-feverish-on-cruise-ship-in-japan |title=1 crew member tests positive, 20 feverish on cruise ship in Japan &#124; ABS-CBN News |publisher=News.abs-cbn.com |date=2020-04-21 |accessdate=2020-04-25}}</ref>

''Costa Atlantica'' had 623 crew members and no passengers at the time the first positive case was first reported.<ref name="atlantica.yahoo" />  There were a total of 56 crew members that have had heavy contact with the positive case.<ref name="atlantica.yahoo" />  They have all been quarantined, and PCR tests have been planned for all of them.<ref name="atlantica.abscbn" /><ref name="atlantica.yahoo" />  [[Nagasaki Prefecture|The prefecture]] has considered requesting assistance from the [[Japan Self-Defense Forces|Self-Defense Forces]] to help manage the situation.<ref name="atlantica.abscbn" />

On 22 April 2020, officials of the prefecture announced that, of the 56 additional tests conducted, an additional 33 crew members had tested positive, bringing the total number of positive cases to 34.<ref name="atlantica.kyodo">{{cite news|url=https://english.kyodonews.net/news/2020/04/5879e08833fd-33-more-crew-on-cruise-ship-docked-in-japan-test-positive-for-virus.html|title=33 more crew on cruise ship docked in Japan test positive for virus|newspaper=[[Kyodo News]]|date=22 April 2020|accessdate=24 April 2020}}</ref> The other 23 tests returned negative.<ref name="atlantica.kyodo" /> On 23 April, it was announced that 48 tests in total have returned positive, with 14 of the positive cases being cooks or people serving food.<ref name="atlantica.reuters.1">{{cite web|url= https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-japan-ship/italian-cruise-ship-in-japan-has-48-coronavirus-cases-idUSKCN22504S|title=Italian cruise ship in Japan has 48 coronavirus cases|publisher=Reuters|date=23 April 2020|accessdate=24 April 2020}}</ref> On 24 April, officials stated that 91 people had tested positive, with one patient being hospitalized.<ref name="atlantica.reuters.2">{{cite web|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-japan-ship/coronavirus-tally-rises-to-91-on-italian-cruise-ship-in-japan-idUSKCN22601Z|title=Ninety-one crew have virus on Italian liner in Nagasaki|publisher=Reuters|date=24 April 2020|accessdate=24 April 2020}}</ref> Officials also noted that even though ''Costa Atlantica'' had been quarantined upon its arrival in Japan, with its crew ordered not to leave the quay unless they needed to visit a hospital, some crew members had left without informing the officials.<ref name="atlantica.reuters.2" />

On 25 April, [[Television Nagasaki]] announced that 57 new cases had been discovered, bringing the total number of positive cases to 148.<ref name="atlantica.fnn">{{cite web |url=https://www.fnn.jp/articles/-/36390 |title=【速報】長崎での客船クラスター 乗組員全員の検査実施 新たに57人感染確認 計148人に |publisher=Fnn.jp |date=25 April 2020 |accessdate=25 April 2020 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200425070437/https://www.fnn.jp/articles/-/36390 |archive-date=25 April 2020 |url-status=dead }}</ref> As of 4 May, the number had increased to 149. Those crew members that tested negative began flying home from Japan on 4 May.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.usatoday.com/story/travel/cruises/2020/05/06/coronavirus-costa-atlantica-flies-some-crew-home-including-american/5174092002/ |title=Costa Atlantica begins flying crew home (including lone American), announces additional coronavirus case |last=Oliver |first=David |work=USA Today |date=6 May 2020 |access-date=4 August 2020}}</ref> On 31 May, after all remaining crew tested negative for the virus, the cruise ship departed Nagasaki for Manila.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.japantimes.co.jp/news/2020/05/31/national/virus-hit-italian-cruise-ship-leaves-nagasaki/ |title=Virus-hit Italian cruise ship leaves Nagasaki |work=The Japan Times |date=31 May 2020 |access-date=4 August 2020}}</ref>

=== ''MSC Seaview'' === <!-- 2020.04.30: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On 30 April 2020, ''{{ill|A Tribuna|pt}}'' reported that the [[National Sanitary Surveillance Agency|Brazilian Health Regulatory Agency]] confirmed the notification of 10 crew members aboard {{ship||MSC Seaview}} that had tested positive for the virus.<ref name="seaview.tribuna">{{cite web|url=https://www.atribuna.com.br/noticias/portoemar/com-10-casos-de-covid-19-msc-seaview-entra-em-quarentena-no-porto-de-santos-1.99148 |title=Com 10 casos de Covid-19, MSC Seaview entra em quarentena no Porto de Santos |publisher=Atribuna.com.br |language=pt |date=2020-04-30 |accessdate=2020-05-04}}</ref>  The ship entered quarantine at the [[Port of Santos]] on the same day, shortly after the notification.<ref name="seaview.tribuna" />

On 5 May 2020, [[Empresa Brasil de Comunicação]] reported that there were 80 confirmed cases of the virus at that point, with another 30 suspected cases, out of a total of 615 crew members aboard.<ref name="seaview.ebc">[https://radioagencianacional.ebc.com.br/geral/audio/2020-05/transatlantico-msc-seaview-tem-80-casos-confirmados-de-covid-19 Transatlântico MSC Seaview tem 80 casos confirmados de Covid-19] RadioagenciaNacional 5 May 2020</ref>  Later that day, the number of confirmed cases rose to 86.<ref name="seaview.tribuna.2">{{cite web|url=https://www.atribuna.com.br/noticias/portoemar/n%C3%BAmero-de-tripulantes-infectados-pelo-coronav%C3%ADrus-no-msc-seaview-sobe-para-86-1.99756|title=Número de tripulantes infectados pelo coronavírus no MSC Seaview sobe para 86|website=A Tribuna}}</ref>

=== ''Mein Schiff 3'' === <!-- 2020.05.01: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On 1 May 2020, [[TUI Cruises]] confirmed that a crew member aboard their ship {{ship||Mein Schiff 3}} had tested positive for the virus.{{efn|The crew member had actually tested positive the day before.<ref name="schiff3.sukf" />}}<ref name="schiff3.tui">[https://www.schiffe-und-kreuzfahrten.de/news/tui-cruises-bestaetigt-corona-fall-auf-mein-schiff-3-in-cuxhaven/203152/ TUI Cruises bestätigt Corona-Fall auf Mein Schiff 3 in Cuxhaven] Schiffe und Keuzfahren</ref>  At the time, the ship was located at [[Cuxhaven]], Germany, with 2899 crew members aboard, a number normally highly unusual for a cruise ship, but was a result of the company deciding to transfer crew members from other ships, including {{ship||Mein Schiff 4}} and {{ship||Mein Schiff 6}}, to this ship.<ref name="schiff3.tui" /><ref name="schiff3.sukf">[https://www.schiffe-und-kreuzfahrten.de/news/corona-fall-auf-der-mein-schiff-3-in-cuxhaven-crewstimmung-generell-nicht-gut/203101/ Corona-Fall auf der Mein Schiff 3 in Cuxhaven – Crewmitglieder äußern sich zur Lage!] Schiffe und Keuzfahren</ref><ref name="schiff3.crew">[https://crew-center.com/mein-schiff-3-one-crew-member-tests-positive-covid-19 Mein Schiff 3: One Crew Member Test Positive for Covid-19] CrewCenter 1 May 2020</ref>  Crew members aboard ''Mein Schiff 3'' have strongly complained about the mismanagement and general cluelessness of those higher up, and about the difficulty of attempting to isolate on such a crowded ship.<ref name="schiff3.sukf" />  It has also been pointed out that TUI Cruises' statement contained factual inaccuracies.<ref name="schiff3.tui" />

By 3 May 2020, the entire crew of ''Mein Schiff 3'' had been tested, with 8 tests returning positive and about a third of the tests still being processed.<ref name="schiff3.sukf.2">{{cite web|url=https://www.schiffe-und-kreuzfahrten.de/news/mein-schiff-3-mindestens-8-weitere-coronafaelle-crew-soll-auf-mein-schiff-6-wechseln/203486/|title=Mein Schiff 3: Mindestens 8 weitere Coronafälle - Crew soll auf Mein Schiff 6 wechseln|date=4 May 2020}}</ref>  The rest of the tests were processed by 6 May 2020, at which point a total of 9 positive cases had been found.<ref name="schiff3.sukf.3">{{cite web|url=https://www.schiffe-und-kreuzfahrten.de/news/mein-schiff-3-weiterer-corona-fall-mittlerweile-9-positive-crewmitglieder/203623/|title=Mein Schiff 3: Weiterer Corona-Fall - mittlerweile 9 positive Crewmitglieder|date=6 May 2020}}</ref>

=== ''MSC Preziosa'' === <!-- 2020.05.01: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On 1 May 2020, CrewCenter reported that two crew members aboard {{ship||MSC Preziosa}} had tested positive for the virus.<ref name="preziosa.crew">[https://crew-center.com/msc-preziosa-2-crew-members-test-positive-covid-19 MSC Preziosa: Two Crew members test positive  for Covid-19] Crew Center 1 May 2020</ref>  The first positive result was announced to the crew on 30 April 2020 and the second on 1 May.<ref name="preziosa.crew" />  The positive results came as a surprise for many of the crew, as no one had boarded the ship since 23 March, well over a month earlier, and all crew members had been isolating themselves in guest cabins since 11 April, nearly three weeks earlier.<ref name="preziosa.crew" />

=== ''Seven Seas Navigator'' === <!-- 2020.05.21: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On 21 May 2020, it was reported that a female crew member aboard {{ship||Seven Seas Navigator}} had tested positive for the virus, and that a second crew member was also showing symptoms of the virus.<ref name="navigator.elpais">{{Cite web|url=https://elpais.com/espana/catalunya/2020-05-21/un-crucero-con-400-pasajeros-en-cuarentena-en-el-puerto-de-barcelona-tras-un-positivo.html|title=Un crucero con 450 ocupantes, en cuarentena en el puerto de Barcelona por dos posibles positivos|first=Blanca|last=Cia|date=21 May 2020|website=EL PAÍS}}</ref><ref name="navigator.crew">{{Cite web|url=https://crew-center.com/seven-seas-navigator-crew-14-day-quarantine|title=Seven Seas Navigator Crew In 14 Day Quarantine &#124; Crew Center|website=crew-center.com}}</ref>  The ship had subsequently requested entry to the [[Port of Barcelona]], and the [[Ministry of Health (Spain)|Ministry of Health]] granted them an exception to do so.<ref name="navigator.elpais" />  After docking, both sick crew members were given [[COVID-19 testing#Serology tests|serological tests]], and both returned positive.<ref name="navigator.elpais" /><ref name="navigator.lavanguardia">{{Cite web|url=https://www.lavanguardia.com/ocio/viajes/20200523/481325761810/cruceros-coronavirus-barcelona-manila.html|title=Los inéditos viajes de los cruceros por el mundo a causa del coronavirus|date=22 May 2020|website=La Vanguardia}}</ref>{{efn|They were also given [[polymerase chain reaction]] [[COVID-19 testing#PCR based|tests]], but no results appear to have been reported as of 2020.05.23.<ref name="navigator.lavanguardia" /><ref name="navigator.crew" />}}  Both crew members have been isolated, and the rest of the roughly 450 crew members of the ship have been placed under quarantine.<ref name="navigator.elpais" /><ref name="navigator.abc">{{Cite web|url=https://www.abc.es/espana/catalunya/abci-tripulantes-crucero-atrapado-covid-estamos-bien-pero-queremos-volver-casa-202005231744_noticia.html|title=Tripulantes del crucero atrapado por el Covid: "Estamos bien, pero queremos volver a casa"|date=23 May 2020|website=abc}}</ref>

=== ''Adventure of the Seas'' === <!-- 2020.05.22: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On 22 May 2020, ''Loop Jamaica'' reported that 5 crew members of {{ship||Adventure of the Seas}} recently repatriated to Jamaica had tested positive for the virus.<ref name="adventure.loop.3">{{Cite web|url=http://www.loopjamaica.com/content/10-more-covid-19-cases-including-5-cruise-ship-falmouth|title=10 more COVID-19 cases, including 5 from cruise ship in Falmouth|website=www.loopjamaica.com}}</ref>  The ship had docked at [[Falmouth, Jamaica|Falmouth]], [[Jamaica]], on 19 May 2020 after drifting in [[Caribbean]] waters waiting for clearance to dock because Jamaica had closed its borders.<ref name="adventure.loop.1">{{Cite web|url=http://www.loopjamaica.com/content/coronavirus-cruise-ship-jamaican-workers-arrives-falmouth|title=Coronavirus: Cruise ship with Jamaican workers arrives in Falmouth|website=www.loopjamaica.com}}</ref><ref name="adventure.national">{{Cite web|url=https://www.caribbeannationalweekly.com/cnw-tv/cnw90-may-20-2020/|title=CNW90 May 20, 2020|date=20 May 2020}}</ref><ref name="adventure.jis">{{Cite web|url=https://jis.gov.jm/ship-workers-arrive-at-falmouth-pier/|title=Ship Workers Arrive At Falmouth Pier|date=20 May 2020|website=Jamaica Information Service}}</ref>  Aboard were 1044 Jamaican crew members, all to be repatriated and tested for the virus, and over 300 crew members who were foreign nationals, who would not be allowed to disembark.<ref name="adventure.jis" /><ref name="adventure.loop.2">{{Cite web|url=http://www.loopjamaica.com/content/over-300-foreigners-ship-falmouth-not-allowed-disembark|title=Over 300 foreigners on ship in Falmouth not allowed to disembark|website=www.loopjamaica.com}}</ref>

By 24 May 2020, 9 crew members in total had tested positive;<ref name="adventure.observer">{{Cite web|url=http://www.jamaicaobserver.com/latestnews/Nine_cruise_workers_test_positive_for_COVID-19_process_continues|title=Jamaica Observer Limited|website=Jamaica Observer}}</ref> by 26 May, 19 in total had tested positive, and 624 negative.<ref name="adventure.loop.4">{{Cite web|url=http://www.loopjamaica.com/content/eight-new-covid-19-cases-total-now-564|title=Eight new COVID-19 cases; total now 564|website=www.loopjamaica.com}}</ref><ref name="adventure.gleaner">{{Cite web|url=http://jamaica-gleaner.com/article/lead-stories/20200526/eight-new-covid-cases-push-tally-564-recoveries-now-267|title=Eight new COVID cases push tally to 564, recoveries now at 267|date=26 May 2020|website=jamaica-gleaner.com}}</ref>

=== ''Mein Schiff 1'' === <!-- 2020.07.21: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On {{dts|2020.07.21|format=dmy}}, ''Cruise Law News'' reported that crew members aboard {{ill|Mein Schiff 1 (2018)|lt=''Mein Schiff 1''|de|Mein Schiff 1 (Schiff, 2018)}} stated that seven crew members had tested positive for the virus.<ref name="schiff1.law">https://www.cruiselawnews.com/2020/07/articles/uncategorized/mein-schiff-1-cruise-reportedly-cancelled-due-to-covid-19</ref>

[[TUI Cruises]] had planned to restart its cruise schedule with a series of "Blue Cruises"<!-- apparently not using the same meaning as that mentioned in the "Blue Cruise" article, which covers cruises in turkey -->, short cruises of a few days in length that made no stops aside from arriving at its port of departure.<ref name="schiff1.crew">https://crew-center.com/tui-cruises-postpones-restart-mein-schiff-1-start-team-not-completed</ref>  ''Mein Schiff 1'' was to have launched from the [[Port of Kiel]] on {{dts|2020.07.31|format=dmy}}, but TUI Cruises cancelled the trip, citing issues assembling a crew in time due to coronavirus travel restrictions.{{r|schiff1.crew}}<ref name="schiff1.sukf">https://www.schiffe-und-kreuzfahrten.de/news/mein-schiff-1-blaue-reise-abgesagt/206799/</ref>  However, ''Cruise Law News'' requested additional information from crew members, and two responded stating that the crew had already been assembled, but the real reason the trip was cancelled was because of the seven positive test results, all from crew members that had only recently joined the crew.{{r|schiff1.law}}  ''Der Kreuzfahrttester'' suggested a third possible reason for the cancellation: TUI Cruises was unable to find enough people willing to work for the company due to how badly the company handled the coronavirus crisis.<ref name="schiff1.tester">https://kreuzfahrttester.com/2020/07/23/blaue-reise-absage/</ref>

The first Blue Cruise aboard ''Mein Schiff 1'' was rescheduled for {{dts|2020.08.03|format=dmy}}.{{r|schiff1.law}}

Eventually, on {{dts|2020.07.29|format=dm}}, TUI Cruises admitted that five crew members had tested positive for the virus.<ref name="schiff1.kfat">https://www.kreuzfahrt-aktuelles.de/news/tui-cruises-5-crewmitgleider-fuer-die-mein-schiff-1-wurden-positiv-auf-das-coronavirus-getestet/7710/</ref><ref name="schiff1.law.02">https://www.cruiselawnews.com/2020/07/articles/uncategorized/finally-the-truth-mein-schiff-1-crew-members-test-positive-for-covid-19/</ref>

=== ''Roald Amundsen'' === <!-- 2020.07.31: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On {{dts|2020.07.31|format=dmy}}, the [[University Hospital of North Norway]] (UNN) announced that four crew members aboard {{MS|Roald Amundsen}} had tested positive for the virus.{{efn|They were the first coronavirus patients admitted to UNN since {{dts|2020.06.05|format=dm}}.{{r|amundsen.nordlys}}}}<ref name="amundsen.unn_hf">https://mobile.twitter.com/UNN_HF/status/1289221203954081792</ref>

Norwegian cruise line [[Hurtigruten AS]] was the first ocean cruise line in the world to resume cruise operations, with {{MS|Otto Sverdrup}} sailing from [[Bergen]] to [[Kirkenes]] on {{dts|2020.06.16|format=dmy}}.<ref name="sverdrup.mapper">https://www.cruisemapper.com/news/7552-first-ocean-cruise-line-to-resume-sailings-is-hurtigruten</ref><ref name="sverdrup.critic">https://www.cruisecritic.com/news/5396/</ref>  Hurtigruten's ''Roald Amundsen'' resumed its cruises on {{dts|2020.07.17|format=dm}} with a seven-day roundtrip cruise from [[Tromsø]] to [[Svalbard]], followed by another that departed on {{dts|2020.07.24|format=dm}}.<ref name="amundsen.avid">https://www.avidcruiser.com/2020/07/hurtigruten-to-resume-operations-on-14-ships/</ref><ref name="amundsen.barents">https://thebarentsobserver.com/en/travel/2020/07/hurtigruten-cancels-svalbard-cruise-crew-members-have-been-diagnosed-covid-19</ref>

Several days before arriving back in Tromsø on {{dts|2020.07.31|format=dm}}, two crew members became sick and were isolated.{{efn|Hurtigruten claimed that the two crew members were isolated for a different illness.{{r|amundsen.vg}}}}<ref name="amundsen.vg">https://www.vg.no/nyheter/innenriks/i/rABORw/smitteutbrudd-paa-hurtigruten-fire-ansatte-innlagt-paa-sykehus</ref>  Upon arrival at Tromsø, they were tested for coronavirus, and both test results were positive.{{r|amundsen.vg}}{{r|amundsen.barents}}  As a result, all 160 crew members were to be tested.<ref name="amundsen.nordlys">https://www.nordlys.no/koronautbrudd-pa-hurtigruten-ligger-til-kai-i-tromso/s/5-34-1335120</ref>

Many passengers had already disembarked and had been making their way home before the news broke about the infected crew, with one bus driver stating that he had driven 28 passengers from ''Roald Amundsen'' to the airport hours before the news broke.{{r|amundsen.nordlys}}  Some passengers stated that they first learned of the news via online news media.{{r|amundsen.barents}}  Hurtigruten stated that they would inform the passengers of both cruises about their potential exposure to the virus via [[SMS]].{{r|amundsen.vg}}  There were 209 passengers aboard the {{dts|2020.07.17|format=dm}} cruise, and 177 aboard the {{dts|2020.07.24|format=dm}} cruise.{{r|amundsen.vg}}

Later that evening, it was revealed that a passenger from [[Vesterålen]] aboard the {{dts|2020.07.17|format=dm}} cruise had tested positive for the virus days earlier, and that on {{dts|2020.07.29|format=dm}}, an official from Vesterålen clearly informed at least four people in Hurtigruten, as well as the [[Norwegian Institute of Public Health]] (NIPH), about the positive case, and recommended that all passengers be informed on the same day.<ref name="amundsen.vg.02">https://www.vg.no/nyheter/innenriks/i/2GLwVR/hurtigruten-ble-varslet-om-passasjer-med-smitte-etter-forrige-tur-mente-det-ikke-var-grunn-til-bekymring</ref>  However, Hurtigruten had believed there was no need to worry.{{r|amundsen.vg.02}}

All 177 passengers aboard the {{dts|2020.07.24|format=dm}} cruise and all 160 crew members were required to enter quarantine.<ref name="amundsen.vg.03">https://www.vg.no/nyheter/innenriks/i/0nMzVE/hurtigruten-passasjer-slipper-ikke-inn-paa-fly-surrealistisk</ref>  ''Roald Amundsen'' was originally scheduled to set sail for Svalbard again that afternoon, but the cruise was cancelled, and the ship's next planned voyage was scheduled for the beginning of September.{{r|amundsen.nordlys}}

The next day, on {{dts|2020.08.01|format=dm}}, Tromsø Mayor {{ill|Gunnar Wilhelmsen|no}} announced that an additional 29 crew members had tested positive, meaning that 33 people had tested positive in total so far.<ref name="amundsen.nordlys.02">https://www.nordlys.no/29-nye-smittetilfeller-pa-roald-amundsen/s/5-34-1335445</ref><ref name="amundsen.law">https://www.cruiselawnews.com/2020/07/articles/disease/covid-19-crew-member-infections-confirmed-on-hurtigruten-cruise-ship/</ref>  Later that evening, Mayor Wilhelmsen confirmed that 36 people had tested positive so far, including one passenger.<ref name="amundsen.vg.04">https://www.vg.no/nyheter/i/na3PwQ/36-hurtigruten-ansatte-bekreftet-smittet</ref>  The mayor disapproved of how Hurtigruten had handled the situation, stating that he believed the passengers should have been informed and quarantined before the ship had docked in Tromsø, and that he worried that a major outbreak might occur because passengers had wandered around the city before they were notified about the sick crew members.{{r|amundsen.vg.04}}  [[Troms]] [[Storting|Parliament]] Member [[Kent Gudmundsen]] expressed shock over Hurtigruten's management of the situation,{{r|amundsen.vg.04}} and [[Minister of Health and Care Services]] [[Bent Høie]] praised the efforts of Tromsø and the NIPH in containing the virus.{{r|amundsen.vg.04}}  Up to 69 [[List of municipalities of Norway|municipalities]] might have been affected by the outbreak, and officials had still been unable to contact 20 of the 177 passengers aboard the {{dts|2020.07.27|format=dm}} cruise by evening.<ref name="amundsen.vg.05">https://www.vg.no/nyheter/innenriks/i/pLoEgo/69-kommuner-fra-hele-landet-er-beroert-av-hurtigruten-utbruddet</ref>{{r|amundsen.vg.04}}

As of 3 August 2020, four of the passengers who were on the two cruises had tested positive for the virus.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/aug/03/two-cruise-ships-hit-by-coronavirus-weeks-after-industry-restarts|title=Two cruise ships hit by coronavirus weeks after industry restarts|date=3 August 2020 |publisher=The Guardian|access-date=2020-08-03}}</ref>

=== ''Paul Gauguin'' === <!-- 2020.08.01: first known report of first positive case, used to order ships chronologically -->

On {{dts|2020.08.01|format=dmy}}, [[Polynésie la 1ère]] reported that a case of the virus had been found aboard [[Paul Gauguin (ship)|MS ''Paul Gauguin'']].<ref name="gauguin.la1ere">https://la1ere.francetvinfo.fr/polynesie/tahiti/cas-positif-covid-ete-detecte-paquebot-croisiere-paul-gauguin-858438.html</ref>  The passengers were told about the case that same day, and the ship immediately turned around, skipping its next port of call in [[Rangiroa]], and headed back toward [[Papeete]].{{r|gauguin.la1ere}}<ref name="gauguin.rfi">https://www.rfi.fr/en/france/20200803-300-people-confined-on-cruise-ship-in-french-polynesia-after-covid-19-case-confirmed</ref>  All the passengers were requested to stay in their cabins while food was brought to them.{{r|gauguin.rfi}}

The ship had left [[Tahiti]] on {{dts|2020.07.30|format=dm}}, and had made a stopover in [[Bora Bora]] before [[Compagnie du Ponant]], owner of ''Paul Gauguin'', was aware of the presence of an asymptomatic case of the virus in a 22-year-old American female passenger<!-- it is unclear whether the passengers or crew were informed of any details about the identity of the positive case, including whether the case was female or male, or a passenger or crew member -->.{{efn|''[[The Guardian]]'' reported that the case was found in a crew member, but many other sources reported that it was found in a female passenger.{{r|gauguin.guardian}}{{r|gauguin.rfi}}{{r|gauguin.seatrade}}{{r|gauguin.today}}<ref name="gauguin.20minutes">https://www.20minutes.fr/sante/2833595-20200803-coronavirus-polynesie-340-personnes-confinees-bord-bateau-croisiere-apres-detection-cas-positif</ref>  [[Seatrade Communications|''Seatrade Cruise News'']] reported that the passenger was tested aboard the ship, following the rule that tourists must be tested within four days after arrival in [[French Polynesia]].{{r|gauguin.seatrade}}}}<ref name="gauguin.sudouest">https://www.sudouest.fr/2020/08/03/polynesie-francaise-un-cas-de-coronavirus-detecte-sur-un-bateau-de-croisiere-340-personnes-confinees-a-bord-7714527-10997.php</ref><ref name="gauguin.guardian">https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/aug/03/two-cruise-ships-hit-by-coronavirus-weeks-after-industry-restarts</ref><ref name="gauguin.today">https://www.usatoday.com/story/travel/cruises/2020/08/03/hurtigruten-covid-19-outbreak-passengers-crew-infected-cruise/5570867002/</ref>  During the stopover, both the passengers and the crew had been able to disembark and interact with the locals of Bora Bora for two days.{{r|gauguin.rfi}}

Once ''Paul Gauguin'' arrived back in Papeete on the morning of {{dts|2020.08.02|format=dm}}, all 148 passengers and 192 crew members were placed in confinement.{{r|gauguin.sudouest}}<ref name="gauguin.seatrade">https://www.seatrade-cruise.com/news/paul-gauguin-cruise-cut-short-covid-19-case-wider-test-results-awaited</ref>  The asymptomatic American was travelling with her mother, who had tested negative, and both were disembarked and escorted to a hotel where they were placed under isolation.{{r|gauguin.seatrade}}{{r|gauguin.today}}

=== ''SeaDream I'' ===
[[File:2017-04-06 01 SEA DREAM I - IMO 8203438.jpg|thumb|''SeaDream I'' in 2017]]
On 11 November 2020, the Government of [[Barbados]] received a request for assistance from [[SeaDream I]]  with reports of a suspected positive case of [[Coronavirus disease 2019|COVID-19]] on board, Six passengers aboard SeaDream I were later confirmed to have been infected with COVID-19.<ref name="GIS131120">{{cite web |title=Sea Dream Is Appreciative Of Barbados’ Assistance |url=https://gisbarbados.gov.bb/blog/sea-dream-is-appreciative-of-barbados-assistance/ |website=The Barbados Government Information Service |publisher=The Government of Barbados |accessdate=14 November 2020 |date=13 November 2020}}</ref><ref name="iWitness1311">{{cite web |title=COVID-19 outbreak on cruise ship while in Grenadines |url=https://www.iwnsvg.com/2020/11/13/covid-19-outbreak-on-cruise-ship-while-in-grenadines/ |website=iWitness News |accessdate=14 November 2020 |date=13 November 2020}}</ref><ref name="Guardian13">{{cite web |title=SeaDream 1: five passengers test positive for Covid-19 on Caribbean cruise ship |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/nov/12/caribbean-cruise-ship-coronavirus-seadream |website=The Guardian |accessdate=16 November 2020 |date=13 November 2020}}</ref> Subsequently there was an additional case recorded. <ref name="GIS141120">{{cite web |title=Seven COVID-19 Cases On SeaDream 1 |url=https://gisbarbados.gov.bb/blog/seven-covid-19-cases-on-seadream-1/ |website=Barbados Government Information Service |accessdate=14 November 2020 |date=14 November 2020}}</ref>

On 15 November 2020 it was reported that one crew member had also tested positive. <ref name="Walker15">{{cite web |last1=Walker |first1=Jim |title=SeaDream Cruise Guests Flown From Barbados to Airports Around the World |url=https://www.cruiselawnews.com/2020/11/articles/disease/seadream-cruise-guests-flown-from-barbados-to-airports-around-the-world/ |website=Cruise Law News |publisher=Walker and O'Neil Maritime Lawyers |accessdate=16 November 2020 |date=15 November 2020}}</ref>

On 17 November 2020 it was reported that 7 guests and two crew members aboard SeaDream 1 tested positive for Covid-19. SeaDream has cancelled all remaining 2020 cruises following the outbreak.<ref name="CNN171120">{{cite web |last1=Hunter |first1=Marnie |last2=Oppmann |first2=Patrick |title=SeaDream cancels remaining 2020 cruises following Covid outbreak |url=https://edition.cnn.com/travel/article/caribbean-cruises-canceled-seadream-covid/index.html |website=CNN |publisher=Cable News Network |accessdate=19 November 2020 |date=17 November 2020}}</ref>

* {{ship||Costa Diadema}}: On 24 March 2020, the ship docked at [[Limassol]], [[Cyprus]], and a crew member suspected of suffering from the coronavirus was taken to hospital. Several other crew members were also reported to be ill. ''Costa Diadema'' was sailing from Dubai to [[Savona]], Italy, without passengers.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus: crew member from Italian cruise liner taken to Limassol hospital |url=https://cyprus-mail.com/2020/03/24/coronavirus-crew-member-from-italian-cruise-liner-taken-to-limassol-hospital/ |accessdate=27 March 2020 |agency=CyprusMail |date=24 March 2020}}</ref>
* {{ship||Golden Princess|2000|2}}: At least three passengers have been quarantined by the ship's doctor, according to local health officials. It was en route for [[Melbourne]] on 18 March 2020.<ref name=autogenerated1>{{cite web |title=Multiple cruise ships are left stranded as coronavirus cases increase |url=https://edition.cnn.com/travel/article/cruise-ships-stranded-coronavirus-trnd/index.html |website=[[CNN]] |first=Christina |last=Zdanowicz |date=18 March 2020 |access-date=25 March 2020 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200327213136/https://edition.cnn.com/travel/article/cruise-ships-stranded-coronavirus-trnd/index.html |archive-date=27 March 2020 |url-status=live }}</ref> As of 1 April 2020, it was docked in Melbourne.<ref name="guardian2020-04-01"/>
* {{MV|Mahabaahu||2}}: Several passengers and crew members were quarantined after an American passenger who have traveled in the ship in [[Brahmaputra River]] in [[Assam]], [[India]], was tested positive in [[Bhutan]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.hindustantimes.com/india-news/foreign-tourists-in-assam-face-hassles-amid-fear-of-coronavirus-spread/story-v8QyfMjs39BOKCZthcL7mJ.html|title=Foreign tourists in Assam face hassles amid fear of coronavirus spread|date=13 March 2020|website=Hindustan Times|language=en|access-date=20 March 2020|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200320083931/https://www.hindustantimes.com/india-news/foreign-tourists-in-assam-face-hassles-amid-fear-of-coronavirus-spread/story-v8QyfMjs39BOKCZthcL7mJ.html|archive-date=20 March 2020|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.guwahatiplus.com/daily-news/coronavirus-outbreak-crew-passengers-of-m-v-mahabaahu-quarantined|title=Coronavirus Outbreak: Crew, Passengers of M V Mahabaahu Quarantined|website=G Plus|language=en|access-date=20 March 2020|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200320083932/https://www.guwahatiplus.com/daily-news/coronavirus-outbreak-crew-passengers-of-m-v-mahabaahu-quarantined|archive-date=20 March 2020|url-status=live}}</ref>
* {{anchor|Marella Dream|MS Marella Dream}} {{MS|Marella Dream||2}} <!-- first reported 2020.03.28 -->: On 28 March 2020, it was announced that a crew member of MS ''Marella Dream'' had died on 27 facing public health dilemma|accessdate=3 July 2020}}</ref>  The crew member was a 48-year-old Indonesian national.<ref name="dream.hoy">{{cite -->he crew member had underlying health issues and had not tested positive for Covid-19 and there are no positive cases of Covid-19 on board the ship", leading sources to conclude that either he had not been tested,{{efn|This is possibly because the spokesperson had not been reported to have stated that the crew member had tested negative.}}<ref name="dream.crew">[https://crew-center.com/crew-member-dies-marella-dream Crew Member dies in on Marella Dream] CrewMember 31 March 2020</ref><ref medical treatment.<ref name="dream.chronicle" />  It was decided to transfer the crew member during daylight hours, around 07:30 the next morning, but the crew member's condition worsened overnight and he passed at 04:47.<ref name="dream.chronicle" />  Subsequently, public health officials refused permission for the disembarkation of the body and the government asked the ship to leave responsibility of [[Malta]], the ship's [[flag state]].<ref name="dream.chronicle" />  At the time of the crew member's death, there were 560{{efn|It is unclear if this number included the recently deceased.}} crew members and no passengers aboard.<ref name="dream.chronicle" />  ''Marella Dream'' later docked in [[Málaga]], [[Spain]], on 28 March, to disembark the deceased crew member.<ref name="dream.hoy" />
* [[File:MSC Magnifica anchored at Garden Island, Western Australia, March 2020 01.jpg|thumb|''MSC Magnifica'' anchored off the coast of Western Australia]] {{anchor|MSC Magnifica}} {{ship||MSC Magnifica}}: [[Premier of Western Australia]] [[Mark McGowan]] claimed that there were 250 suspected cases on board, while MSC Cruises' claimed that all aboard were in good health.<ref name="magnifica.watoday" /><ref name="newsweek.status" />  It was later conjectured that this was a result of miscommunication, as 250 passengers had "visited the medical room in the past two weeks", for issues such as painkillers and [[dressing (medical)|dressings]], by 23 March 2020, when the ship was heading for [[Fremantle]], [[Australia]] to disembark patients to hospitals and isolation.<ref 23 March 2020|url-status= live}}</ref> Before reaching Fremantle, ''MSC Magnifica'' had been able to let a few hundred passengers off in Sydney and Melbourne, "under strict conditions", but the cruise ship was denied entry into Western Australia.<ref>{{cite web |title= WA resists cruise ship with sick on board |url= subsequently denied entry to Dubai and was still in the Perth area on 25 March.<ref>{{cite 2020|url-status=live}}</ref> It eventually set sail for Sri Lanka, where, on 6 April, the vessel made a "technical stop" in [[Colombo]].<ref name="magnifica.bbc" />  Here, a 75-year-old female German passenger with heart problems who needed urgent care and a Sri Lankan chef was allowed to disembark.<ref>{{cite |publisher=dailymirror.lk |date=6 April 2020 |access-date=6 April 2020 }}</ref>  The German passenger subsequently died.<ref name="magnifica.bbc"/>  On 20 April 2020, ''MSC Magnifica''<!-- "MSC" is part of the name of the ship --> docked in [[Marseille]], France, letting out all its passengers and terminating the cruise.<ref name="magnifica.industry">{{cite web | title=Last Cruise Ship at Sea no passengers and no crew members had shown any coronavirus symptoms.<ref name="magnifica.industry" />
* {{ship||MSC Musica||2}}: On 2020.04.29, ''{{ill|A Tribuna|pt}}'' reported that a 32-year-old Indian crew member of ''MSC Musica'' had tested positive for the coronavirus.<ref name="musica.tribuna">{{cite web|url=https://www.atribuna.com.br/noticias/portoemar/tripulante-do-msc-musica-contrai-coronav%C3%ADrus-em-santos-e-navio-entra-em-quarentena-1.99016|title=Tripulante do MSC Musica contrai coronavírus em Santos e navio entra em quarentena|website=A Tribuna}}</ref>  The crew member was initially admitted to hospital for emergency care due to anemia, and had tested negative for the virus upon admission.<ref name="musica.tribuna" />  However, when the crew member was scheduled for discharge, another test was performed, which returned positive.<ref name="musica.tribuna" />  It is unclear if the virus was contracted aboard the ship or after disembarkation, but ''MSC Musica'', which had been moored at the [[Port of Santos]], was placed under quarantine as a preventative measure, with the standard 14 days of quarantine beginning on the day the crew member had disembarked.<ref name="musica.tribuna" />
* [[File:Norwegian gem in Sicily 2008.jpg|thumb|''Norwegian Gem'' in 2008]]{{ship||Norwegian Gem}}:
** On 13 April 2020, a 56-year-old Filipino male crew member died aboard ''Norwegian Gem''.<ref name="gem.law.2">[https://www.cruiselawnews.com/2020/05/articles/disease/covid-cover-up-ncl-ship-doctor-on-the-norwegian-gem-dies/ COVID COVER-UP? NCL Ship Doctor on the Norwegian Gem Dies] Cruise Law News 1 May 2020</ref>  The crew member had been treated for pneumonia and [[arrhythmia#Tachycardias|tachycardia arrhythmia]].<ref name="gem.insider">[https://www.businessinsider.com/norwegian-cruise-line-doctor-dies-on-gem-ship-2020-5 A doctor has died on the Norwegian Gem, two weeks after crew members saw another body loaded into an ambulance] Business Insider 2 May 2020</ref>  [[Norwegian Cruise Line]] (NCL) claimed they did not believe he was infected with the virus, but appeared to have not offered any explanation as to why an autopsy was not performed, or why he was not tested for the virus.<ref name="gem.law.2" />  He was disembarked at Miami by people in [[hazmat suit]]s.<ref name="gem.insider" />
** On 23 April, NCL sent a letter to the crew members aboard stating that another crew member, who was on the cruise ship between 31 March 2020 and 14 April, had tested positive for the virus.<ref name="gem.law.1">[https://www.cruiselawnews.com/2020/04/articles/disease/cruise-covid-19-norwegian-gem-crew-member-tested-positive-for-coronavirus/ Cruise COVID-19: Norwegian Gem Crew Member Tested Positive for Coronavirus] Cruise Law News 25 April 2020</ref>  Notably, this letter was not sent to crew members who were no longer on the ship.<ref name="gem.law.1" />{{efn|It has been conjectured that this was because those crew members would have been entitled to certain benefits had they been infected with the virus while on board.<ref name="gem.law.1" />}}
** On the morning of 30 April, the senior doctor on ''Norwegian Gem'' was found dead in his cabin.<ref name="gem.law.2" />  NCL claimed that he died of a heart attack in his sleep, though crew members stated that he was being treated for pneumonia and had not been tested for the virus.<ref name="gem.law.2" />  Also, according to crew members, a nurse who had worked closely with the doctor had reportedly tested positive for the virus after being removed from the ship.<ref name="gem.law.2" /><ref name="gem.insider" />  There was concern among crew members that NCL had been hiding evidence of the virus on board ''Norwegian Gem'', which may become an issue if NCL carries out plans to combine crews from different ships together before sailing them back home.<ref name="gem.law.2" />

=== No currently suspected cases ===
<!-- ordered alphabetically -->
* {{ship||AIDAaura}}: The German cruise ship ''AIDAaura'', with about 1,200 people on board, was held on 3 March 2020 in the harbour of [[Haugesund]], [[Norway]], while two asymptomatic German passengers were tested who had been in contact with a person who subsequently developed COVID-19; their test results were negative.<ref name=berliner>{{cite web|url=https://www.morgenpost.de/vermischtes/article228600469/Coronavirus-Corona-Kreuzfahrtschiffe-Ministerium-warnt-Deutsche-vor-Kreuzfahrten.html|title=Coronavirus: Außenministerium warnt Deutsche vor Kreuzfahrten|language=de|trans-title=Coronavirus: crisis team advises against cruises|newspaper=Berliner Morgenpost|date=5 March 2020|access-date=5 March 2020|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200306052600/https://www.morgenpost.de/vermischtes/article228600469/Coronavirus-Corona-Kreuzfahrtschiffe-Ministerium-warnt-Deutsche-vor-Kreuzfahrten.html|archive-date=6 March 2020|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.thelocal.de/20200303/coronavirus-german-cruise-ship-held-in-norwegian-harbour-as-passengers-tested|title=Coronavirus: German cruise ship held in Norwegian harbour as passengers tested|date=3 March 2020|accessdate=3 March 2020|newspaper=The Local De|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200303133842/https://www.thelocal.de/20200303/coronavirus-german-cruise-ship-held-in-norwegian-harbour-as-passengers-tested|archive-date=3 March 2020|url-status=live}}</ref>
* {{anchor|AIDAblu}} {{ship||AIDAblu}}: On 18 May 2020, a male Filipino crew member of ''AIDAblu'' was found dead in his cabin.<ref name="aidablu.crew">{{cite web|url=http://crew-center.com/filipino-crew-member-found-dead-his-cabin-aida-cruise-ship|title=Filipino Crew Member Found Dead in His Cabin on Aida Cruise Ship &#124; Crew Center|website=crew-center.com}}</ref>  He had worked in the ship's [[galley (kitchen)|galley]] department.<ref name="aidablu.crew" />  The ship was docked in Hamburg at the time.<ref name="aidablu.crew" />  The crew member was not suspected to have died of COVID-19.<ref name="aidablu.crew" />  During the previous week, 188 crew members of ''AIDAblu'' had been successfully repatriated from Germany to the Philippines, though it is unclear why the deceased was not among them.<ref name="aidablu.law">{{cite web|url=https://www.cruiselawnews.com/2020/05/articles/disease/filipino-galley-employee-dies-on-aidablu/|title=Filipino Galley Employee Dies on AIDAblu|date=19 May 2020|website=Cruise Law News}}</ref><ref name="aidablu.pcg">{{cite web|url=https://frankfurtpcg.de/ph-consulate-general-in-frankfurt-assists-repatriation-of-239-filipino-seafarers|title=PH Consulate General in Frankfurt Assists Repatriation of 239 Filipino Seafarers|website=frankfurtpcg.de}}</ref>  In addition, many employees working for [[AIDA Cruises]] have praised the company for their transparency and honesty since the start of the pandemic, as well as the care that their managers have shown for their mental health.<ref name="aidablu.crew" />
* {{ship||AIDAmira}}: Six passengers on the ship were isolated in the middle of March, after flying on a plane with a sailor who later tested positive with the virus.<ref name="aidamira.times" />  More than 1,700 were trapped on the cruise ship, docked at [[Cape Town]], [[South Africa]], pending test results.<ref name="aidamira.times">{{cite web|title= 1,700 trapped on Cape Town cruise ship in Covid-19 drama|url= https://www.timeslive.co.za/news/south-africa/2020-03-17-1700-trapped-on-cape-town-cruise-ship-in-covid-19-drama/|website= The Sunday Times|date= 18 March 2020|access-date= 18 March 2020|archive-url= https://web.archive.org/web/20200318012422/https://www.timeslive.co.za/news/south-africa/2020-03-17-1700-trapped-on-cape-town-cruise-ship-in-covid-19-drama/|archive-date= 18 March 2020|url-status= live}}</ref>  By 2020.03.19, all tests returned negative, and passengers were allowed to disembark.<ref name="aidamira.arabia">{{cite web|url=https://cruisearabiaonline.com/2020/03/19/aidamira-cleared-of-coronavirus-in-cape-town-as-sa-shuts-down-cruise-operations/|title=AIDAmira cleared of Coronavirus in Cape Town as SA shuts down cruise operations|first=Shaun|last=Ebelthite|date=19 March 2020|website=cruisearabiaonline.com}}</ref>
* {{ship||Anthem of the Seas}}: On 7 February 2020, the ship was quarantined because a passenger from the 27 January 2020 sailing had traveled through mainland China. The CDC reported on 8 February 2020 that the guest tested negative, and the ship was cleared to sail on 10 February 2020. All 5,000 passengers due to sail on 7 February had to find their own arrangements for lodging and ended up sailing to Bermuda for four days instead of the Bahamas for eight.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://newjersey.news12.com/story/41679605/anthem-of-the-seas-cruise-ship-sets-sail-from-bayonne-after-coronavirus-scare|title=Anthem of the Seas cruise ship sets sail from Bayonne after coronavirus scare|website=newjersey.news12.com|language=en|access-date=12 February 2020}}</ref>
* {{anchor|Carnival Breeze}} {{ship||Carnival Breeze}}: On 9 May 2020, it was reported that a 29-year-old Hungarian crew member aboard ''Carnival Breeze'' had been found dead in his cabin, reportedly due to suicide.<ref name="breeze.crew">[http://crew-center.com/crew-member-reportedly-commits-suicide-carnival-breeze Crew Member Reportedly Commits Suicide on Carnival Breeze] CrewCenter 9 May 2020</ref>  He was an assistant shore excursion manager, and was last seen with someone on 6 May.<ref name="breeze.crew" />  A crew member blamed depression due to long periods of isolation aboard the ship, while others were shocked because things seemed normal with the crew member.<ref name="breeze.crew" />  At the time, ''Carnival Breeze'' was crossing the Atlantic Ocean heading toward [[Southampton]], England, to repatriate its European crew members.<ref name="breeze.crew" /><ref name="breeze.law">{{cite web|url=https://www.cruiselawnews.com/2020/05/articles/disease/crew-member-dies-on-the-carnival-breeze-during-final-repatriation-cruise/|title=Crew Member Dies on the Carnival Breeze During Final Repatriation Cruise|date=10 May 2020|website=Cruise Law News}}</ref>
* {{ship||Carnival Panorama}}: On 7 March 2020, the [[Centers for Disease Control and Prevention]] (CDC) halted passengers disembarking from the cruise ship ''Carnival Panorama'' docked at [[Long Beach, California|Long Beach]] Cruise Terminal in California when a female passenger was reported to be sick.<ref name="lbpost.1">{{cite web |title=UPDATE: Coronavirus test comes back negative • Long Beach Post News |url=https://lbpost.com/news/cdc-coronavirus-cruise-ship-testing-carnival-panorama |website=lbpost.com |access-date=8 March 2020 passenger was transported to a hospital to be tested, and all passengers were held on board the ship pending test results.<ref>{{cite web |title=Official City Statement from the City of Long Beach Regarding Carnival Cruise Ship |url=http://longbeach.gov/press-releases/official-city-statement-from-the-city-of-long-beach-regarding-carnival-cruise-ship/ |website=longbeach.gov |access-date=8 March 2020 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200403230813/http://longbeach.gov/press-releases/official-city-statement-from-the-city-of-long-beach-regarding-carnival-cruise-ship/ |archive-date=3 April 2020 |url-status=live }}</ref><ref name=Twitter-1236401838682804225>{{cite web |url= https://mobile.twitter.com/LongBeachCity/status/1236401838682804225 |work= @LongBeachCity |author= City of Long Beach |date= 7 March 2020 |publisher= Twitter |title= 1236401838682804225 }}</ref>  The test came back negative late that evening, and disembarkation was scheduled to resume the next morning.<ref name="lbpost.1" /> ''Carnival Panorama'' was returning from a trip to Mexico with scheduled stops at [[Cabo San Lucas]], [[Mazatlán]] and [[Puerto Vallarta]], which were also scheduled stops for ''Grand Princess'' during the previous month.<ref name="lbpost.1" /><ref>{{cite web |title=Carnival Cruises 2019–2020 |url=https://www.carnivalcruiseline.is/sites/default/uploads/catalogue/CCL_2019_2020_Katalog_IS/mobile/index.html#p=39 |website=carnivalcruiseline.is |pages=38–39 |access-date=8 March 2020 |url-status=live }}</ref><ref name="brochure">{{cite web |title=2019–2020 Hawaii, Mexico & California coast |url=https://book.princess.com/images/cc/brochure/downloads/hi-mex-cal-coast-brochure-2019-20-v2.pdf |website=book.princess.com |access-date=7 March 2020
